function info($str) { echo "INFO: $str\n"; }
function warn($str) { echo "WARNING: $str\n"; }
function err($str) { die("FATAL ERROR: $str\n"); }

@set_time_limit(0);

@header('Content-Type: text/plain');

chdir(__DIR__);
if (trim(@file_get_contents('oidplus_version.txt')) !== 'Revision 61') {
	err('This update can only be applied to OIDplus version 2.0.0.61!');
}

if (version_compare(PHP_VERSION, '7.0.0') < 0) {
	err('You need PHP Version 7.0 to update to this version');
}

// Dir added: doc
@mkdir('doc');
if (!is_dir('doc')) {
	warn('Directory could not be created: doc');
} else if ((DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR === '/') && !@chmod('doc', 0755)) {
	warn('Could not change directory permissions of doc');
}

// File added: doc/INFO
function writefile_1() {
	@$fp = fopen('doc/INFO', 'w');
	@fwrite($fp, base64_decode('CkhUTUwgZmlsZXMgd2hpY2ggYXJlIGFkZGVkIGluIHRoaXMgZGlyZWN0b3J5IGFyZSBhZGRlZCB0byB0aGUgIkRvY3VtZW50cyIgc2VjdGlvbiBpbiB5b3VyIE9JRHBsdXMgc3lzdGVtLgoKWW91IGNhbiBkZWZpbmUgY3VzdG9tIGljb25zIGJ5IHBsYWNpbmcgdGhl'));
	@fwrite($fp, base64_decode('IGZpbGVzIC4uLl9iaWcucG5nIGFuZCAuLi5fdHJlZS5wbmcKClRoZSBIVE1MIGhlYWRsaW5lIHdpbGwgZGVmaW5lIHRoZSB0aXRsZSBvZiB0aGUgbWVudSBlbnRyeQoK'));
	@fclose($fp);
}
if (is_file('doc/INFO') && (sha1_file('doc/INFO') != 'c548cd9b53aafc3a1f04eeb5d969eb242daf2803')) {
	warn('File was created by someone else. Will overwrite the changes now: doc/INFO');
	$tmp = pathinfo('doc/INFO');
	$backup_name = $tmp['dirname'].DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR.$tmp['filename'].'.'.date('Ymdhis',@filemtime('doc/INFO')).(isset($tmp['extension']) ? '.'.$tmp['extension'] : '');
	warn('Creating a backup as '.$backup_name);
	if (!@copy('doc/INFO', $backup_name)) {
		warn('Creation of backup failed');
	}
}
writefile_1();
if (!is_file('doc/INFO')) {
	warn('File cannot be created (not existing): doc/INFO');
} else if (sha1_file('doc/INFO') != 'c548cd9b53aafc3a1f04eeb5d969eb242daf2803') {
	warn('File cannot be created (checksum mismatch): doc/INFO');
} else if ((DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR === '/') && !@chmod('doc/INFO', 0644)) {
	warn('Could not change file permissions of doc/INFO');
}

if (is_file('doc/acknowledgements.html') && (sha1_file('doc/acknowledgements.html') != 'f7b539ad555f6b63a9b8e18a3d51e024db8c0a78')) {
	warn('File was created by someone else. Will overwrite the changes now: doc/acknowledgements.html');
	$tmp = pathinfo('doc/acknowledgements.html');
	$backup_name = $tmp['dirname'].DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR.$tmp['filename'].'.'.date('Ymdhis',@filemtime('doc/acknowledgements.html')).(isset($tmp['extension']) ? '.'.$tmp['extension'] : '');
	warn('Creating a backup as '.$backup_name);
	if (!@copy('doc/acknowledgements.html', $backup_name)) {
		warn('Creation of backup failed');
	}
}
writefile_2();
if (!is_file('doc/acknowledgements.html')) {
	warn('File cannot be created (not existing): doc/acknowledgements.html');
} else if (sha1_file('doc/acknowledgements.html') != 'f7b539ad555f6b63a9b8e18a3d51e024db8c0a78') {
	warn('File cannot be created (checksum mismatch): doc/acknowledgements.html');
} else if ((DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR === '/') && !@chmod('doc/acknowledgements.html', 0644)) {
	warn('Could not change file permissions of doc/acknowledgements.html');
}

	writefile_12();

		warn('File cannot be created (not existing): TODO');
	} else if (sha1_file('TODO') != 'b7f151ba0b892258b7913754c6a0682b2bc47738') {
		warn('File cannot be created (checksum mismatch): TODO');
	} else if ((DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR === '/') && !@chmod('TODO', 0644)) {
		warn('Could not change file permissions of TODO');
	}
} else {
	if (@sha1_file('TODO') !== 'b7f151ba0b892258b7913754c6a0682b2bc47738') {
		if (@sha1_file('TODO') !== '5df37173a3bd2369b046ffaa70f2505ea789fd4d') {
			warn('File was modified. Will overwrite the changes now: TODO');
			$tmp = pathinfo('TODO');
			$backup_name = $tmp['dirname'].DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR.$tmp['filename'].'.'.date('Ymdhis',@filemtime('TODO')).(isset($tmp['extension']) ? '.'.$tmp['extension'] : '');
			warn('Creating a backup as '.$backup_name);
			if (!@copy('TODO', $backup_name)) {
				warn('Creation of backup failed');
			}
		}
		writefile_12();
		if (@sha1_file('TODO') !== 'b7f151ba0b892258b7913754c6a0682b2bc47738') {
			warn('File cannot be written (checksum mismatch): TODO');
		}
	}
}

if (!is_file('dev/country_getter')) {
	warn('File has vanished! Will re-create it: dev/country_getter');
	writefile_13();
	if (!is_file('dev/country_getter')) {
		warn('File cannot be created (not existing): dev/country_getter');
	} else if (sha1_file('dev/country_getter') != '6124ffad5b47f50069247361aecfc5aeca19ce9f') {
		warn('File cannot be created (checksum mismatch): dev/country_getter');
	} else if ((DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR === '/') && !@chmod('dev/country_getter', 0755)) {
		warn('Could not change file permissions of dev/country_getter');
	}
} else {
	if (@sha1_file('dev/country_getter') !== '6124ffad5b47f50069247361aecfc5aeca19ce9f') {
		if (@sha1_file('dev/country_getter') !== '9c8e1754fd14833275a627a10381d2df613561b0') {
			warn('File was modified. Will overwrite the changes now: dev/country_getter');
			$tmp = pathinfo('dev/country_getter');
			$backup_name = $tmp['dirname'].DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR.$tmp['filename'].'.'.date('Ymdhis',@filemtime('dev/country_getter')).(isset($tmp['extension']) ? '.'.$tmp['extension'] : '');
			warn('Creating a backup as '.$backup_name);
			if (!@copy('dev/country_getter', $backup_name)) {
				warn('Creation of backup failed');
			}
		}
		writefile_13();
		if (@sha1_file('dev/country_getter') !== '6124ffad5b47f50069247361aecfc5aeca19ce9f') {
			warn('File cannot be written (checksum mismatch): dev/country_getter');
		}
	}
}
